function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/_overview');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/_overview');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/_overview') != 'f9f320e9bf5bcf113ecca3030357cfc26800c227') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/_overview', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/_overview');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== 'f9f320e9bf5bcf113ecca3030357cfc26800c227') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== 'aa4ae55ad87b7a2398572e0b1b07e8df75bbfbf7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/_overview');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/_overview');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/_overview')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/_overview', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== 'f9f320e9bf5bcf113ecca3030357cfc26800c227') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') != 'a3af9fcdaf7803574681e08a5cfde5394ce33ea2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'a3af9fcdaf7803574681e08a5cfde5394ce33ea2') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'd01415a1eadde32e60940c9d75287f72e3d6b821') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php') !== 'a3af9fcdaf7803574681e08a5cfde5394ce33ea2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/gmp_supplement.inc.php');
		}
	}

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php') !== 'ddd0600bdd39a537bd25de042ef1d0cd9c847144') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv4_functions.inc.php');

if (!is_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') != '8a44c5d7ec08d798adc67868336713e142c59abe') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '8a44c5d7ec08d798adc67868336713e142c59abe') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '5b0d4ac34e0995dc86650333df53cd0a28c5f093') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php') !== '8a44c5d7ec08d798adc67868336713e142c59abe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/ipv6_functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') != '3dada3da91bc5763acca7ccca93296a3ceda87d4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '3dada3da91bc5763acca7ccca93296a3ceda87d4') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '65aac6b8303ff5f7b2bb6c7d49d0f2175466e3aa') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oid_utils.inc.php');

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oid_utils.inc.php') !== '3dada3da91bc5763acca7ccca93296a3ceda87d4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oid_utils.inc.php');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') != '2ffb0e74f34ccf6e0be5801e197aea2aacc4dea2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '2ffb0e74f34ccf6e0be5801e197aea2aacc4dea2') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '27c5191ecffb5a09b7d766fb9c534b12ed5f35d7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/uuid_utils.inc.php') !== '2ffb0e74f34ccf6e0be5801e197aea2aacc4dea2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/uuid_utils.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '1135b504c9ce1c0b16ff69e012159c686c2037af') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '1135b504c9ce1c0b16ff69e012159c686c2037af') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'efcd706824731a4972a253a635911147f34c1aa7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '1135b504c9ce1c0b16ff69e012159c686c2037af') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.min.css.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.css.php');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.css.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') != 'e3b42004151fbcd1c5d155e8885125090d71bb10') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.css.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.css.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== 'e3b42004151fbcd1c5d155e8885125090d71bb10') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== 'b68cec8924860ce878e6b765cc9a7aa1effdb1df') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.css.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.css.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.css.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.css.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== 'e3b42004151fbcd1c5d155e8885125090d71bb10') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') != '8615a5f97b594bb853b0877f9ab035b0477f7dfd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') !== '8615a5f97b594bb853b0877f9ab035b0477f7dfd') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') !== '92ed332d5a1f1dde35faf635a0caf73fe701dfc8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionMySQLi.class.php') !== '8615a5f97b594bb853b0877f9ab035b0477f7dfd') {

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '03a9fb62a3d95cd64ed769aa974978ce89b0cb1d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '03a9fb62a3d95cd64ed769aa974978ce89b0cb1d') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '7976a544d7dacbb51eabc90574e1b3d6d4417886') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '03a9fb62a3d95cd64ed769aa974978ce89b0cb1d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
